They used to collect grain from Buckinghamshire farmers, and deliver them to milling companies at the London docks for processing. The lorries returned from London loaded with the processed animal feed to sell onto local farmers. I am kneeling at front right.', The Greenway, Secondary Modern School',  updated their cover photo.',   ', 11 September 2013',   ', The Greenway, Secondary Modern School',  updated their cover photo.',   ', 11 September 2013',   ', The Greenway, Secondary Modern School',   ', 7 September 2013',   ', u"It's good to hear everyone posting with their memories of the school. I used to live in Nursery Waye, opposite the RAF Station, my walk to school was along the busy Uxbridge Road. I remember Stephen Carsons, Roland Pengelly, and Thomas Jefferson, as friends. Uxbridge in the early sixties seemed to have an identity of it's own in those days. Boyhood memories of those days were; the GWR line into Vine Street station, the steam tank engines, and the diesel railcars, the demolition of the station, and subsequent lifting of the tracks. I hated PE, especially the cross country running through the lanes at the back of the school, where Brunel University now is located. Interestingly my first job, was as an apprentice electrician at Brunel during it's construction.", The Greenway, Secondary Modern School',   ', 5 April 2013',   ', Torrevieja, Spain',   ', I started school here in Sept 1962, and left at Easter 1966. You could cycle through the smaller bore of the tunnel then, as this was for pedestrians, and cyclists. Loved watching the BEA Viscount, and Vanguard turbo props, and the BEA Tridents, my favourite though was the BOAC VC10, with it's four rear mounted jet engines. The new Boeing 707 was also to be seen in the early 1960's. Did anyone else enjoy plane spotting?", The Greenway, Secondary Modern School',   ', 19 January 2014',   ', u"Found this photo from 1957, this was an Uxbridge firm of seed merchants, E.E. Chaney. They used to collect grain from Buckinghamshire farmers, and deliver them to milling companies at the London docks for processing. The lorries returned from London loaded with the processed animal feed to sell onto local farmers. If anyone has any photos of The Greenway School, or indeed any historical photos of Uxbridge during the 50's, and 60's, it would be good to see them published.", The Greenway, Secondary Modern School',   ', 11 September 2013',   ', Found a photo of Vine Street station online. I am kneeling at front right.', The Greenway, Secondary Modern School',  updated their cover photo.',   ', 11 September 2013',   ', The Greenway, Secondary Modern School',  updated their cover photo.',   ', 11 September 2013',   ', The Greenway, Secondary Modern School',   ', 7 September 2013',   ', u"It's good to hear everyone posting with their memories of the school. I used to live in Nursery Waye, opposite the RAF Station, my walk to school was along the busy Uxbridge Road. I remember Stephen Carsons, Roland Pengelly, and Thomas Jefferson, as friends. Uxbridge in the early sixties seemed to have an identity of it's own in those days. Boyhood memories of those days were; the GWR line into Vine Street station, the steam tank engines, and the diesel railcars, the demolition of the station, and subsequent lifting of the tracks. I hated PE, especially the cross country running through the lanes at the back of the school, where Brunel University now is located. Interestingly my first job, was as an apprentice electrician at Brunel during it's construction.", The Greenway, Secondary Modern School',   ', 5 April 2013',   ', Torrevieja, Spain',   ', I started school here in Sept 1962, and left at Easter 1966. Other memories, are hot coke stoves, bottled milk, and outside toilets.', See more', Situated in The Greenway, Uxbridge, Middx.
